***schrift.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrift.html>schrift</a> (9297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scrift</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scricht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skrifti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scrīptum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrift.html>schrift</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schriften.html>schriften</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schriftje.html>schriftje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>script</li>
<li>notebook</li>
<li>scripture</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Not to be confused with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrift.html>Schrift</a></i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a different meaning ("Bible" rather than "scripture") and a different gender (feminine rather than neuter).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***schrijven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrijven.html>schrijven</a> (814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schriven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">scrīvan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrībaną</i>, a late borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scrībō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrijven.html>schrijven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to write

***schroef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schroef.html>schroef</a> (15018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">escroue</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schroef.html>schroef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schroeven.html>schroeven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schroefje.html>schroefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>screw (fastener)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A ship's propeller.</li>
<li>An Archimedes screw.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common in the Netherlands. In Belgium <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijzen.html>vijs</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common.

***schuchter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuchter.html>schuchter</a> (41583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>Via</a> Early Modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schüchter</i> from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> source. The contemporary German form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schüchtern</i>. Eventually akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">scheu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuw.html>schuw</a></i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shy</i>.
</p>

***schudden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schudden.html>schudden</a> (2813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schudden.html>schudden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">scudden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skudjaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schütten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the iterative <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schütteln</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schudden.html>schudden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shake, to tremble, to waver</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shuffle (cards)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nod as in to express disagreement</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schulen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skūlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skūlijaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">schûlen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schūlen</i> (obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schaulen</i>).

***schuim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuim.html>schuim</a> (10103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schuum</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schum</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skūm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skūmaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schaum</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuim.html>schuim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuimen.html>schuimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuim.html>schuimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>foam, froth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a type of spongy <a href = vnd.unilang:sweets.html>sweets</a>, made of albumen and sugar <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as a countable object always diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>scum, rabble, crooks</li>
<li>impurity, flaw, especially in (molten) metal</li></ol>

***schuimen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuimen.html>schuimen</a> (53286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schumen</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuim.html>schuim</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuimen.html>schuimen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to foam, to produce foam.
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, Vreni <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Jong-Müggler amp; Irmela Kelling, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gezond.html>Gezond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:kookboek.html>kookboek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volwaardig.html>volwaardige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a> Christofoor, 45.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:herhaaldelijk.html>Herhaaldelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhit.html>verhit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frituurvet.html>frituurvet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donkerder.html>donkerder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleur.html>kleur</a>, stroperig, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuimen.html>schuimen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruikt.html>ruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onaangenaam.html>onaangenaam</a>.
<dl><dd>Repeatedly heated frying oil <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> a darker colour, becomes viscid, <a href = vnd.unilang:starts.html>starts</a> to <b>foam</b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:smells.html>smells</a> unpleasantly.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remove foam</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remove impurities from something.
<ul><li><b>1944</b>, Andries <a href = vnd.unilang:anton.html>Anton</a> Verdenius, <i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlandse taaltuin: <a href = vnd.unilang:wandeling.html>wandelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarnemingen.html>waarnemingen</a></i>, Elsevier, 110.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a> <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouwden.html>bouwden</a>, <b>schuimden</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overbodige.html>overbodige</a> bastaardwoorden, <a href = vnd.unilang:bouwden.html>bouwden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:edel.html>edel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:organisme.html>organisme</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepste.html>diepste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedachten.html>gedachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fijnste.html>fijnste</a> gemoedsschakeringen <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> verklanken.
<dl><dd>Our <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> of science <b><a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> away</b> and built, they <b>removed</b> unnecessary bastardized <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> from the language, built them into a noble organism, that could express the most profound thoughts and most delicate shades of mood into <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<dl><dd>But <a href = vnd.unilang:pirates.html>pirates</a> from all nations <b>plundered</b> in this area, and roamed these <a href = vnd.unilang:seas.html>seas</a> and those, who cam from the <i>Hava(h)<a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i>, from <i>Jamaica</i>, <i>Saint <a href = vnd.unilang:domingo.html>Domingo</a></i> or the more distant <i>Bay of Campeche</i> always feared these treacherous islands.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rummage, to scour.
<ul><li><b>2015</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:margriet.html>Margriet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>Linden</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefde.html>liefde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i>, Querido.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oma.html>oma</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>Griet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spannende.html>spannende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uren.html>uren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> M in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kasten.html>kasten</a> <b>‘<a href = vnd.unilang:schuim.html>schuim</a>’n’</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oma.html>oma</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>Griet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noemde.html>noemde</a>.
<dl><dd>Granny <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>Griet</a>'s house, and particularly the parts upstairs, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> full of new and exciting <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, M could <b>rummage</b> in the closets for <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>, as granny <a href = vnd.unilang:griet.html>Griet</a> called it.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wander, to roam [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> <span>(<a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>/object)</span></span>]

<p>Origin uncertain. annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">skean</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slanting, sloping</span><span ***schuit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuit.html>schuit</a> (19555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skūta</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuit.html>schuit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuiten.html>schuiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuitje.html>schuitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A boat or small ship, usually a flat-bottomed one used for inland navigation or less commonly for coastal navigation; a barge.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schout</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skult</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skuldiz</i>.

***schuren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuren.html>schuren</a> (21493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuren.html>schuren</a></i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">escurer</i>.  More at <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scour</i>, a borrowing from Middle Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuren.html>schuren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grate, rub, scour, chafe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sand</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">afschuren</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">schuring</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">schuurder</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuurpapier.html>schuurpapier</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuur.html>schuur</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuren.html>schuren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring in, notably a crop to the barn</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schutting.html>schutting</a> (22425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schuttinge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schut.html>schutten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shield, protect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schutting.html>schutting</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuttingen.html>schuttingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schutting.html>schuttinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a (usually wooden) solid, or nearly solid, barrier separating two pieces of <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>; fence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschutting.html>beschutting</a></span></li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuren.html>schuren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papier.html>papier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***schwarz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schwarz.html>schwarz</a> (72999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">swarz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">swarz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*swartaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swordo-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dirty, dark, black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwart.html>zwart</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swart</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swarthy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">swart</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sort</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schwarz.html>schwarz</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">schwärzer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am schwärzesten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>black, reflecting little or no light</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> illegal</li>
<li>black, having a high amount of melanin in an organ, e.g. the skin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany" class="extiw" title="w:Germany">Germany</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pertaining to the CDU or CSU (large center-right Christian Democratic parties, whose associated colour <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> black)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of coffee</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> without milk</li>
<li>pertaining to <a href = vnd.unilang:goth.html>Goth</a> music or culture (called <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schwarze.html>schwarze</a> Szene</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black scene</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in German)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scrabble.html>scrabble</a> (22719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schrabbelen</i>, frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schrabben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scrape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scrab</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-le</i>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scrape</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scrabble.html>scrabble</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">scrabbles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">scrabbling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">scrabbled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To scrape or scratch powerfully with hands or claws.
<ul><li><b>1898</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J._Meade_Falkner" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J. Meade Falkner">J. Meade Falkner</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moonfleet" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moonfleet">Moonfleet</a> Chapter 4
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> there <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> no answer, except the echo of my own voice sounding hollow and far off down in the vault. So in despair I <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> back to the earth wall below the slab, and <b>scrabbled</b> at it with my <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a>, till my <a href = vnd.unilang:nails.html>nails</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> broken and the blood <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> out; having all the while a sure knowledge, like a cord twisted round my head, that no effort of mine could ever dislodge the great stone.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1908</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenneth_Grahame" class="extiw" title="w:Kenneth Grahame">Kenneth Grahame</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wind_in_the_Willows" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Wind in the Willows">The Wind in the Willows</a></cite>, London |  Wordsworth Classics, published 1993, page 12:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">So he scraped and scratched and <b>scrabbled</b> and scrooged, then he scrooged again[.]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To gather hastily.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To move with difficulty by making rapid movements back and forth with the hands or paws.
<dl><dd><i>She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> on her hands and knees <b>scrabbling</b> in the mud, <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> for her missing wedding <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To scribble.
<ul><li>Bible, 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a>. xxi. 13
<dl><dd>David <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <b>scrabbled</b> on the <a href = vnd.unilang:doors.html>doors</a> of the gate.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mark with irregular lines or <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a>; to scribble on.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scrabble.html>scrabble</a></b> paper</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hardscrabble</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">scrabbler</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A scramble.
<dl><dd><i>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scrabble.html>scrabble</a></b> for dear life</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
